! Title: Facebook Zuckestion Killer
! Version: 201901172220
! Author: kowith337
! Homepage: https://github.com/kowith337/PersonalFilterListCollection/blob/master/filterlist/facebook
! Expires: 2 days
! Mirror: https://gitlab.com/kowith337/PersonalFilterListCollection/raw/master/filterlist/facebook/FacebookZuckestionKiller.txt
! Note  : These rules below are pulled from "Thai Paranoid Block" that have some rules that I've created for hide and remove
!         zuckestions, ads, related contents, also remove ability to link back to related application from Facebook, such as
!         Instagram, MESSenger, even Facebook Lite.
! Note 2: Some rules below are too long due to use an xpath, or multiple procedural chaining to make sure it won't accidentally
!         remove something that really need.
! Note 3: Inspired from report on https://github.com/collinbarrett/FilterLists/issues/282

! Give the warning if you're using Facebook on some cellular data provider that can redirect to smartphone-focused site,
! not an actual version of it!
! e.g. when you want to go 'mbasic.faecbook.com' for super lightweight Facebook mobile version, but you get redirected to
! 'm.facebook.com' or 'mobile.facebook.com' then show the suggestion page to use Facebook under "Free Basics" campaign,
! Note: I don't know why it redirected to "h.facebook.com" under non-HTTPS? first before bouncing back to "m.facebook.com"
! or "mobile.facebook.com" ? so, I will blocking it!
! Update: I will keep blocking this, no matter what, when and why...
! Note: Sometime you're able to still use 'm.facebook.com' or 'touch.facebook.com' on mobile data,
!       but it still make xhr to 'mobile.facebook.com', so it's good to block that!
! Furthermore: I HATE FreakBasics by Facebook, internet.org also...
||0.facebook.com$important
||edge-z-*.facebook.com$important
||edge-z-*.facebook.net$important
||edge-z-*.fbcdn.net$important
||facebook.com/zero/policy$document,important
||free.facebook.com$important
||freebasics.com$important
||h.facebook.com$important
||internet.org$important
||mobile.facebook.com$important
||o.facebook.com$important
||web.facebook.com$document,important
||z-m-*.facebook.com$important
||z-m-*.facebook.net$important
||z-m-*.fbcdn.net$important

! It's no need to load anything that not matter to use, because `mbasic.facebook.com` can work fine without JavaScript,
! Inline script, iframe and third party resources.
||$inline-script,domain=mbasic.facebook.com
||$script,domain=mbasic.facebook.com
||$subdocument,domain=mbasic.facebook.com
||$websocket,domain=mbasic.facebook.com

! SOUND annoyances
! This may break sounds in messages, but I have no choice about this, because Facebook Touch site is now play some sounds
! when pick reactions (Like, Love, Haha, etc.), and found AdGuard base are whitelist rsrc.php from fbcdn.net, so I've
! use some wildcard to make sure it will not block something that not related to "M4A audio"
||fbcdn.net/rsrc.php/*.m4a$media,important,domain=m.facebook.com|touch.facebook.com

! Once you've redirect to "Free Basics" prompt page (for example https://m.faccebook.com/zero/policy/optin) these rules below
! will remove the details of "Free Basics" service (descriptyion, legal link) and "Accept" button, only leave "Cancel" button to
! make sure you didn't accidentally accept the terms and apply their "Free Basics" service at all!

! Test Cookie Messing (Now it's caveat because scriptlet cannot remove cookies on the root domain {higher level + HTTP only})
! Remove NoScript State and then set NoScript cookie state to disable
facebook.com##script:inject(cookie-remover.js, noscript)
facebook.com##script:inject(nanop-easy-set-cookie.js, noscript=0)

! Remove referer cookie
facebook.com##script:inject(cookie-remover.js, x-referer)

! This let Facebook forgot mobile carrier name that saved in this cookie (It will keep up to 3 days if you're not remove manuall)
! You can test in 'https://m.facebook.com/diagnostics' and then see the "DATR" value, it should be blank once you've connected to
! private network, such as Ethernet / LAN / Wi-Fi to prevent "Free Basics" menu keep injecting in bookmarks menu
facebook.com##script:inject(cookie-remover.js, datr)
!#endif

! This let Facebook forgot mobile carrier name that saved in this cookie (It will keep up to 3 days if you're not remove manuall)
! You can test in 'https://m.facebook.com/diagnostics' and then see the "DATR" value, it should be blank once you've connected to
! private network, such as Ethernet / LAN / Wi-Fi to prevent "Free Basics" menu keep injecting in bookmarks menu
facebook.com##script:inject(cookie-remover.js, datr)

! You can test in 'https://facebook.com/diagnostics' and then see the "DATR" value, it should be blank once you've connected to
! private network, such as Ethernet / LAN / Wi-Fi to prevent "Free Basics" menu keep injecting in bookmarks menu
facebook.com##script:inject(cookie-remover.js, datr)

! private network, such as Ethernet / LAN / Wi-Fi to prevent "Free Basics" menu keep injecting in bookmarks menu
facebook.com##script:inject(cookie-remover.js, datr)

! This let Facebook forgot mobile carrier name that saved in this cookie (It will keep up to 3 days if you're not remove manuall)
! You can test in 'https://m.facebook.com/diagnostics' and then see the "DATR" value, it should be blank once you've connected to
! private network, such as Ethernet / LAN / Wi-Fi to prevent "Free Basics" menu keep injecting in bookmarks menu
m.facebook.com##script:inject(cookie-remover.js, datr)

! make sure you didn't accidentally accept the terms and apply their "Free Basics" service at all!

! Test Cookie Messing (Now it's caveat because scriptlet cannot remove cookies on the root domain {higher level + HTTP only})
! Remove NoScript State and then set NoScript cookie state to disable

! Remove referer cookie
mbasic.facebook.com##script:inject(cookie-remover.js, x-referer)

! This let Facebook forgot mobile carrier name that saved in this cookie (It will keep up to 3 days if you're not remove manuall)
! You can test in 'https://mbasic.facebook.com/diagnostics' and then see the "DATR" value, it should be blank once you've connected to
! private network, such as Ethernet / LAN / Wi-Fi to prevent "Free Basics" menu keep injecting in bookmarks menu
mbasic.facebook.com##script:inject(cookie-remover.js, datr)

[uBlock Origin 1.17.5.7]
! Title: Facebook Zuckestion Killer
! Version: 201901172220
! Author: kowith337
! Homepage: https://github.com/kowith337/PersonalFilterListCollection/blob/master/filterlist/facebook
! Expires: 2 days
! Mirror: https://gitlab.com/kowith337/PersonalFilterListCollection/raw/master/filterlist/facebook/FacebookZuckestionKiller.txt
! Note  : These rules below are pulled from "Thai Paranoid Block" that have some rules that I've created for hide and remove
!         zuckestions, ads, related contents, also remove ability to link back to related application from Facebook, such as

! This let Facebook forgot mobile carrier name that saved in this cookie (It will keep up to 3 days if you're not remove manuall)
! You can test in 'https://web.facebook.com/diagnostics' and then see the "DATR" value, it should be blank once you've connected to
! private network, such as Ethernet / LAN / Wi-Fi to prevent "Free Basics" menu keep injecting in bookmarks menu
web.facebook.com##script:inject(cookie-remover.js, datr)

! This let Facebook forgot mobile carrier name that saved in this cookie (It will keep up to 3 days if you're not remove manuall)
! You can test in 'https://zero.facebook.com/diagnostics' and then see the "DATR" value, it should be blank once you've connected to
! private network, such as Ethernet / LAN / Wi-Fi to prevent "Free Basics" menu keep injecting in bookmarks menu
zero.facebook.com##script:inject(cookie-remover.js, datr)

! Remove NoScript State and then set NoScript cookie state to disable
mobile.facebook.com##script:inject(cookie-remover.js, noscript)
mobile.facebook.com##script:inject(nanop-easy-set-cookie.js, noscript=0)

! Remove referer cookie
mobile.facebook.com##script:inject(cookie-remover.js, x-referer)

! This let Facebook forgot mobile carrier name that saved in this cookie (It will keep up to 3 days if you're not remove manuall)
! You can test in 'https://mobile.facebook.com/diagnostics' and then see the "DATR" value, it should be blank once you've connected to
! private network, such as Ethernet / LAN / Wi-Fi to prevent "Free Basics" menu keep injecting in bookmarks menu
mobile.facebook.com##script:inject(cookie-remover.js, datr)
!#endif

! This help for opt out zuckestions, you can convert scriptlets below as bookmarklet.
! var divs = document.querySelectorAll('a[data-sigil*="xout"] i.touched_hide'); for (i = 0; i < divs.length; ++i) {divs[i].click();};
